10076-8{_}5641{_}"It looks very greedy, but when can I have a check?
10076-8{_}5642{_}You see, I'm nearly bankrupt."

10076-8{_}5646{_}Then she signed to one of the young men she had sent off.
10076-8{_}5647{_}"Since you are very business-like, you had better have a witness!

10076-8{_}5650{_}The sneer was Ellen's Parthian shot.

10076-8{_}5654{_}Cartwright had won by a few minutes and was satisfied, although he had given Mrs. Seaton twelve-and-sixpence for her shares, when perhaps he need not.

10076-8{_}5657{_}Barbara saw the launch start, with mixed emotions.
10076-8{_}5658{_}She was something of a rebel and had anybody but Cartwright ordered her to stop she would not have obeyed.
10076-8{_}5659{_}She waited in the shade, fixing her eyes on the laboring tugs.
10076-8{_}5660{_}Sometimes she felt a thrill of triumph because Lister had conquered; sometimes she was tortured by suspense.
10076-8{_}5661{_}She did not know if he stood at the levers in the engine-room, or lay, unconscious, in his bunk.
10076-8{_}5662{_}Well, she would soon know and she shrank.
10076-8{_}5663{_}She rubbed the glasses and looked again.
10076-8{_}5664{_}There were two towropes; _Terrier_ plunged across the rollers on _Arcturus'_ starboard bow, the Spanish tug to port.
10076-8{_}5665{_}It looked as if the wreck's steering-gear did not work.

10076-8{_}5667{_}A few minutes afterwards she swung round the mole and Barbara thought the picture moving.
10076-8{_}5668{_}The tugs looked very small; the half-loaded hull they towed to an anchorage floated high above her proper water-line.

10076-8{_}5672{_}Barbara pictured the exhausted men scraping feebly when the sea was calm and the sun did not touch the vessel's side.
10076-8{_}5673{_}All the same, the men had won a triumph.
10076-8{_}5674{_}It looked impossible that the handful of bemused ruffians she had seen start at Liverpool could have dragged the big vessel from the bottom of the lagoon, but the thing was done.

10076-8{_}5678{_}Cartwright had weathered the storm, but she had helped.

10076-8{_}5766{_}My luck has turned and I rather think I can break the opposition."

10076-8{_}5770{_}Lister was delirious, and for two or three days the doctors doubted his recovery.

10076-8{_}5772{_}Next morning they admitted that he was slowly making progress.

10076-8{_}5777{_}She was highly strung and rebellious.
10076-8{_}5778{_}Lister had sent her a message, but she was not allowed to see him yet.
10076-8{_}5779{_}She wanted to see him and was persuaded that for him to see her would not hurt.
10076-8{_}5780{_}She knew he wanted her.
10076-8{_}5781{_}The moon was bright, but the shadow of the hotel stretched across the garden.
10076-8{_}5782{_}Somebody was moving about in the gloom and Barbara started when she saw it was the nurse.
10076-8{_}5783{_}The tired woman had gone out to rest for a few minutes in the cool night air and Barbara saw her opportunity.
10076-8{_}5784{_}Stealing across the veranda, she went along a passage and up some stairs.
10076-8{_}5785{_}The landing at the top was dark, but she knew Lister's door, and turning the handle quietly, looked in.
10076-8{_}5786{_}Bright moonlight shone through the open window and a curtain moved in the gentle breeze.
10076-8{_}5787{_}Mosquito gauze wavered about the bed where a quiet figure lay.
10076-8{_}5788{_}Barbara stole across the floor and pulled back the guard.
10076-8{_}5789{_}The rings rattled and Lister opened his eyes.
10076-8{_}5790{_}He smiled, and Barbara, kneeling by the bed, put her arm round his neck.
10076-8{_}5791{_}"My dear!
10076-8{_}5792{_}You know me?"
10076-8{_}5793{_}"Of course!
10076-8{_}5794{_}I wanted you.
10076-8{_}5795{_}Since I got my senses back, I've tried to call you."
10076-8{_}5796{_}"You called not long since.
10076-8{_}5797{_}I cheated the nurse and came; but if you ought to be quiet, I mustn't talk.
10076-8{_}5798{_}The doctors said--"  "They don't understand," said Lister.
10076-8{_}5799{_}"Now I have seen you, I'm going to get well."
10076-8{_}5800{_}Barbara lifted her head and studied him.
10076-8{_}5801{_}His face was pinched, his skin was very white and wet.
10076-8{_}5802{_}Her eyes filled and she was moved by tender pity.
10076-8{_}5803{_}"Oh, my dear!"
10076-8{_}5804{_}she said.
10076-8{_}5805{_}"It was for my sake you went!"
10076-8{_}5806{_}Lister took her hand, and she felt his was thin and hot.
10076-8{_}5807{_}"I'm paid for all!
10076-8{_}5808{_}But, Barbara, I think you're _logical_ When I'm better--?"
10076-8{_}5809{_}She kissed him.
10076-8{_}5810{_}"Of course.
10076-8{_}5811{_}I'll marry you when you like.
10076-8{_}5812{_}In the meantime you're weak and tired and must go to sleep."
10076-8{_}5813{_}"I am tired," he admitted.
10076-8{_}5814{_}"Besides, the nurse will come."
10076-8{_}5815{_}Barbara gently touched his wet hair and moved his pillow.
10076-8{_}5816{_}"The nurse is not important, but you mustn't talk."
10076-8{_}5817{_}She gave him her hand again and he went to sleep.
10076-8{_}5818{_}Some time afterwards the nurse returned and started when she saw the white figure kneeling by the bed.
10076-8{_}5819{_}Then she began to talk angrily in a low voice.
10076-8{_}5820{_}Barbara was getting cramped, but without moving her body, she looked at the nurse and her eyes sparkled with rebellious fire.
10076-8{_}5821{_}"Be quiet; he mustn't wake!"
10076-8{_}5822{_}she said.
10076-8{_}5823{_}"There's no use in arguing.
10076-8{_}5824{_}I mean to stay!"
